BYAS NAS DUR KHROD NA BZHUGS PA'I DKYIL 'KHOR GYI DBANG PHYUG LA
DUR KHROD KYI TSUL GYIS GAR BYA ZHING, DAM TSIG KYANG

'DI RNAMS TE DAM TSIG GI NGES PA 'BA' ZHIG BYA'O, ,DE THAMS CAD

'JIGS PAR BYED PAR LHA YI BDAG PO PHYOGS KYI GLANG PO LA GNAS
SHING,

NAS NOR RGYAS NI, ,DKAR PO GDENGS KA BDUN DANG LDAN PA'O CHU
'DZIN STUG PO GTUM DRAG CES BYA CHEN PO NI, ,DRAG PO'I RDZU
'PHRUL CHE LDAN DKAR PO GLANG PO'I GDONG CAN SHI RI shA YI SHING
LA GNAS, ,BYANG DU GNOD SBYIN

DANG, ,DBYUG PA YANG DAG LDAN PA'O 'JOG PO DMAR PO DE BZHIN 'UR
'UR BYED PA'I 'KHOR BYED DE, ,DPAL LDAN BYANG CHUB SHING LA MCHE
GCIG MI YI GDONG CAN BSIL BA NYID 'DIR TSANG TSING LA KHRIGS,

SOGS PA RNAMS KYI SNGAGS SO, ,DPA' BO'I 'DUG STANGS LA RDO RJE
KHRO BO LA SOGS PA RNAMS KYI PHYAG RGYA BYAS TE, LAG PA GNYIS
KYIS KHU TSUR BYAS NAS, GUNG MO'I RTZE MO DANG MING MED KYANG DE
BZHIN DU RDO RJE BSDAMS PA LA GNAS PA DANG, MDZUB MO DAG 'KHYIL
PA'I RNAM

PAS BCINGS PA MTHE BONG LA MNGON PAR PHYOGS PAS CUNG ZAD YON PO'I
RNAM PAR BKUG PA NI GSHIN RJE MTHAR BYED KYI'O, ,G-YON PA KHRO
BO'I KHU TSUR SNYING GAR BZHAG STE, G-YAS PA'I 'GRAM PA LAG PAR
BRDEG PA'I RNAM PAR BSLANG BA NI GZHAN GYIS MI THUB PA'I'O, ,LAG

GI MDUD PAR BCINGS TE MDZUB MO DAG GI RTZE MO SBYAR BA YONGS SU
BSKOR NAS SMIN PHRAG DU GZUNG BA NI RTA MGRIN GYI'O, ,MTHE BONG
DAG GIS MTHE CHUNG GI SEN MO MNAN TE SOR MO LHAG MA RNAMS RDO
RJE'I MTSAN NYID CAN DPUNG PAR

RDO RJE BSDAMS PAS MCHAN KHUNG GI RTZA BAR GZUNG BA NI BDUD RTZI
'KHYIL PA'I'O, ,AOm YA M'ANTA KRi TA H'Um, AOm PRADZNY'ANTA KRi
TA H'Um, AOm PADM'ANTA KRi TA H'Um, AOm AA MRi TA KUndA LI
BIGHN'ANTA KRi TA H'Um, ZHES PA NI GSHIN RJE MTHAR BYED LA SOGS
PA RNAMS KYI PHYAG RGYA'I SNGAGS SO, BZANG PO'I

'DUG STANGS LA NI BYAMS PA LA SOGS PA RNAMS KYI PHYAG RGYA BCA'
STE, RDO RJE KHU TSUR GNYIS BCINGS NAS MDZUB MO DANG MTHE BONG
GUNG MO RNAMS SO SOR PHAN TSUN MNGON DU PHYOGS PAS N'A GA GE SAR
GYI ME TOG DANG 'DRA BAR GZUNG BA NI BYAMS PA'I'O, ,THAL MO YANG
DAG PAR SBYAR

LA BUM PA DMAR PO DANG MDA' SER PO DANG MDA' SNGON PO'O, ,'DIR GO
RIMS JI LTA BA BZHIN DU SHAR LA SOGS PA'I SGO RNAMS KYI NGOS
GNYIS KYI SNAM BU RNAMS LA MTSAN MA GNYIS GNYIS SO, ,SHAR LA SOGS
PA'I SGOR NYI MA

RNAMS LA GSHIN RJE MTHAR BYED DANG GZHAN GYIS MI THUB PA DANG RTA
MGRIN DANG BDUD RTZI 'KHYIL PA RNAMS KYI RAL GRI YU BA NAG PO CAN
DANG RDO RJE SER PO DANG RDO RJE DBYUG PA DMAR PO DANG RAL GRI YU
BA NAG PO CAN NO, ,DBANG LDAN LA SOGS PA'I MTSAMS SU NYI MA RNAMS
LA MI G-YO BA DANG 'DOD PA'I

RGYAL PO DANG DBYUG SNGON CAN DANG STOBS PO CHE RNAMS KYI RAL GRI
DANG RDO RJE SNGON PO DANG RDO RJE'I DBYUG PA SNGON PO'O, ,GSHIN
RJE GSHED KYI MTSAN MA'I PHYI NGOS SU NYI MA LA GNOD MDZES KYI
RAL GRI STE, RTA MGRIN GYI MTSAN MA'I PHYIR NGOS SU NYI MA LA RDO
RJES 'OG GI RDO RJE LCAGS KYU'O, ,ZLA BA DANG NYI MA

THAMS CAD KYI 'OG TU SNA TSOGS 'DAM SKYES TE SNAM BU RNAMS LA NI
BUM PA'O, ,KHA CIG TU NI GSHIN RJE GSHED KYI MTSAN MA'I PHYI NGOS
SU NYI MA LA GTZUG TOR 'KHOR LOS SGYUR BA'I 'KHOR LO DANG, DE'I
PHYI NGOS SU GNOD MDZES KYI RAL GRI'O ZHES GSUNGS SO, ,CHOS KYI
DBYINGS GSUNG

GI DBANG PHYUG GI DKYIL 'KHOR LA NANG GI 'KHOR LO RDUL TSON DKAR
POS DGANG BAR BYA STE, GZHAN RNAMS NI SNGA MA BZHIN NO, ,NANG GI
DKYIL 'KHOR GYI DBUS SU SNA TSOGS PADMA'I LTE BAR ZLA BA LA 'JAM
PA'I DBYANGS KYI RAL GRI YU BA SER PO CAN NO, ,SHAR LA SOGS PA
DANG DBANG LDAN LA SOGS PA'I

SOGS PA BZHIN NI SER MO

PADMA'I DRIL BU 'DZIN BA STE MKHA'

CAN NO, ,SKU'I 'KHOR LO'I DPA' BO RNAMS NI DKAR PO 'KHOR LO DANG

SDIGS MDZUB DANG BCAS PA'I 'KHOR LO 'DZIN PA'O, ,DPA' BO THAMS
CAD YUM LA

RNAMS NI DE'I BRLA GNYIS LA 'KHRIL BA'I TSUL LO, ,KHRA GDONG MA
LA SOGS PA NI G-YAS PA SDIGS MDZUB DANG BCAS PA'I GRI GUG 'DZIN
PA STE LHA MO THAMS CAD PHYAG G-YON PAS THOD PA 'DZIN PA'O,

RJE GUR GYI NANG DU CHOS 'BYUNG GI SNYING POR GZHAL YAS KHANG GI
DBUS SU SNA TSOGS PADMA 'DAB MA BRGYAD PA'I LTE

BAR ZLA BA LA BCOM LDAN 'DAS RDO RJE SGROL MA GSER GYI MDOG LTA
BU SANGS RGYAS LNGA'I COD PAN CAN, RTZA BA DANG G-YAS PA DANG
RGYAB DANG G-YON PA'I ZHAL BZHI GSER GYI MDOG DANG, DKAR PO DANG
SNGON PO DANG DMAR PO'O, ,PHYAG BRGYAD MA G-YAS PA RNAMS KYIS RDO
RJE DANG ZHAGS PA DANG MDA' DANG DUNG RNAMS 'DZIN PA,

G-YON PA RNAMS NI AUTPALA SER PO DANG GZHU DANG LCAGS KYU DANG
SDIGS MDZUB CAN NO, ,SHAR GYI 'DAB MA LA ME TOG SGROL MA DKAR MO
PHYAG DAG GIS ME TOG GI PHRENG BA 'DZIN PA DANG, LHOR BDUG SBOS
SGROL MA NAG MO PHYAG DAG GIS BDUG SBOS KYI SNOD 'DZIN PA DANG,
NUB TU MAR ME SGROL MA SER MO

PHYAG GNYIS KYIS MAR ME'I KONG BU 'DZIN PA DANG, BYANG DU DRI
CHAB SGROL MA DMAR MO PHYAG GNYIS KYIS DRI CHAB KYI DUNG CHOS
'DZIN PA STE LHA MO BZHI PO 'DI RNAMS KYANG ZLA BA LA GNAS PA'O,
,ME LA SOGS PA'I 'DAB MA RNAMS LA RNAM PAR SNANG MDZAD LA SOGS
PA'I NGO BO DE DAG LTA BU'I 'KHOR LO DANG RDO RJE DANG

PADMA DANG RAL GRI'O, ,RIM PA GNYIS PA LA SGO RNAMS SU SHAR DU
RDO RJE LCAGS KYU MA DKAR MO PHYAG G-YAS PAS LCAGS KYU 'DZIN PA
DANG, LHOR RDO RJE ZHAGS PA MA SER MO PHYAG G-YAS PAS ZHAGS PA
'DZIN PA DANG, NUB TU RDO RJE LCAGS SGROG MA DMAR MO PHYAG G-YAS
BAS RDO RJES MTSAN PA'I LCAGS SGROG

@137B 'DZIN PA DANG, BYANG DU RDO RJE DRIL BU MA LJANG GU PHYAG
G-YAS PAS RDO RJE DRIL BU 'DZIN PA'O, ,ME LA SOGS PA'I MTSAMS

DANG ME THAB DANG RGYAL MTSAN CHEN PO'O, ,STENG

'DZIN PA STE, 'OG TU GNOD MDZES MA SNGON MO KLU'I ZHAGS PA 'DZIN
PA'O, ,LHA MO BCU DRUG PO 'DI RNAMS NI PHYAG G-YON PA SDIGS MDZUB
DANG BCAS PA STE SNA TSOGS PADMA DANG NYI MA LA GNAS PA'O, ,BCU
PO 'DI RNAMS KYANG ZHAL GCIG

PA PHYAG GNYIS MA'O, ,BCU GCIG PO RNAMS KYANG RDO RJE SKYIL KRUNG
CAN GSER GYI RNA CHA G-YO BA, RNAM PA SNA TSOGS PA'I GOS DANG RIN

RTEN GYI PHUG GI SNYING POR SNA

ZHING G-YON BRKYANG BAS GNAS PA'I BCOM LDAN 'DAS MA 'OD ZER CAN

RTEN GYIS BRGYAN PA RNAM PA SNA TSOGS PA'I RIN PO CHE'I RGYAN

PHYAG BRGYAD PA G-YAS PA RNAMS KYIS RDO RJE DANG DBYUG PA DANG

BSGRENG BA NI GNOD MDZES KYI PHYAG RGYA'O, ,'OG TU RDO RJES

'OG SNGON PO PHYAG DRUG PA G-YAS PA RNAMS KYIS RDO RJE DANG LCAGS
KYU DANG MDA' 'DZIN ZHING, G-YON PA RNAMS KYIS NU MA DANG ZHAGS
PA DANG BCAS PA'I RTZE GCIG PA DANG GZHU 'DZIN PA'O, ,BGEGS MTHAR
BYED LA SOGS PA BDUN NI RTZA BA DANG G-YAS PA DANG G-YON PA'I
ZHAL GSUM SNGON PO

KYI THUGS KA'I SA BON NI MU:'O, ,AOm AA AA: SARBA TA TH'A GA T'A
HRi DA YA HA RA HA RA, AOm H'Um HR'I: BHA GA W'A NA DZNY'A NA M'U
RTI W'A G'I SHVA RA, MA H'A BA TZA, SARBA DHA RMA GA GA NA AA MA
LA SU PA RI SHUDDHA DHA RMA DH'A TU DZNY'A NA GRBHA AA: ZHES PA
SNYING PO'I SNGAGS SO, ,AOm

AA MRI TA KUndA LI BHI GHN'ANHA KA H'Um, ZHES PA BDUD RTZI 'KHYIL
PA'I SNGAGS TE LAS THAMS CAD PA'O, ,NGAN SONG YONGS SU SPYOD PA'I
DKYIL 'KHOR NI RDO RJE GUR GYI NANG DU RLUNG DANG ME DANG CHU
DANG SA DANG RI RAB KYI STENG GI GZHAL YAS KHANG GI DBUS SU, NANG
GI DKYIL 'KHOR 'KHOR LO RTZIBS BRGYAD PA SER PO,,

RDO RJE PHRED BA SNGON POS YONGS SU BSKOR BA STE 'GA' ZHIG 'KHOR
LO RTZIBS BRGYAD PA SNGON POR GSUNGS LA, GZHAN DU NI 'DI'I 'KHOR
LO'I LTE BA SNGON PO DANG, RTZIBS RNAMS KYI SHAR DKAR PO DANG,
LHO NAG PO DANG, NUB DMAR PO DANG, BYANG LJANG GU'O ZHES GSUNGS
SO, ,'KHOR LO'I LTE PAR SNA TSOGS PADMA LA

GNAS PA'I SENG GE'I STENG DU, BCOM LDAN 'DAS SH'AKYA SER GE RNAM
PAR SNANG MDZAD CHEN PO GSER GYI MDOG CAN CHOS KYI 'KHOR LO'I
PHYAG RGYA MDZAD PA'O, ,SHAR GYI RTZIBS LA RDO RJE GTZUG TOR DKAR
PO SA GNON GYI PHYAG RGYA CAN NO, ,LHO'I RTZIBS LA RIN CHEN GTZUG
TOR SNGON PO MCHOG SBYIN GYI PHYAG

RGYA CAN NO, ,NUB KYI RTZIBS LA PADMA GTZUG TOR DMAR PO BSAM GTAN
GYI PHYAG RGYA CAN NO, ,BYANG GI RTZIBS LA SNA TSOGS GTZUG TOR
LJANG GU MI 'JIGS PA RAB TU SBYIN PA'O, ,ME'I RTZIBS LA GZI BRJID
GTZUG TOR DKAR DMAR 'DRES PA'I MDOG CAN PHYAG G-YAS PAS NYI MA
'DZIN CING, G-YON

@153A *, ,PA DKUR BRTEN PA'O, ,BDEN BRAL GYI RTZIBS LA RGYAL
MTSAN GTZUG TOR DMAR PO DANG 'DRES PA'I NAG PO PHYAG DAG GIS YID
BZHIN GYI NOR BU'I RGYAL MTSAN 'DZIN PA'O, ,RLUNG GI RTZIBS LA
RNON PO'I GTZUG TOR NAM MKHA' LTAR SNGO BSANGS PHYAG G-YAS PA RAL
GRI DANG G-YON PAS

PO TI 'DZIN PA'O, ,DBANG LDAN GYI RTZIBS LA GDUGS CAN GTZUG TOR
DKAR PO PHYAG DAG GIS GDUGS 'DZIN PA'O, ,RDO RJE PHRENG BA'I PHYI
ROL ME LA SOGS PA'I MTSAMS RNAMS SU SGEG MO DANG PHRENG BA DANG
GLU MA DANG GAR MA RNAMS NI, DKAR MO DANG SER MO DANG DMAR MO
DANG, SNA TSOGS KYI MDOG

CAN PHYAG GNYIS MA'O, ,SNAM BU RNAMS LA SGO'I G-YON DU BYANG CHUB
SEMS DPA' GNYIS DANG G-YAS GNYIS TE, DE YANG SHAR GYI SNAM BU LA
BYAMS PA SER PO G-YAS PAS KLU SHING GI ME TOG DANG, G-YON PAS
SPYI BLUGS 'DZIN PA DANG, MTHONG PA DON YOD SER PO PHYAG G-YAS
PAS SPYAN DANG BCAS

PA'I PADMA 'DZIN ZHING, G-YON PA'I KHU TSUR DKUR BRTEN PA DANG,
NGAN SONG KUN 'DREN DKAR PO PHYAG GNYIS KYIS LCAGS KYU 'DZIN PA
DANG, MYA NGAN DANG MUN PA THAMS CAD NGES PAR 'JOMS PA'I BLO GROS
DKAR SER BSRES PA'I MDOG CAN PHYAG G-YAS DBYUG PA 'DZIN ZHING,
G-YON PA'I KHU TSUR

BKUR BRTEN PA'O, ,LHO PHYOGS SU SPOS KYI GLANG PO DKAR LJANG
G-YAS PAS DRI'I DUNG CHOS 'DZIN ZHING, G-YON PA'I KHU TSUR DKUR
BRTEN PA DANG, DPA' BAR 'GRO BA DKAR PO G-YAS PA RAL GRI 'DZIN
ZHING, G-YON PA'I KHU TSUR DKUR BRTEN PA DANG, NAM MKHA'I MDZOD
DKAR SER G-YAS PA PADMA LA

GNAS PA'I CHOS KYI MDZOD 'DZIN ZHING, G-YON PA'I KHU TSUR DKUR
BRTEN PA DANG, YE SHES TOG SNGON PO PHYAG G-YAS PA YID BZHIN GYI
NOR BU'I RGYAL MTSAN 'DZIN ZHING, G-YON PA'I KHU TSUR DKUR BRTEN
PA'O, ,NUB TU BDUD RTZI'I 'OD DKAR PO G-YAS PA COD PAN GYI STENG
DU BDUD RTZI'I BUM PA 'DZIN

ZHING, G-YON PA'I KHU TSUR DKUR BRTEN PA DANG, ZLA BA'I 'OD DKAR
PO G-YAS PA PADMA LA GNAS PA'I ZLA BA'I GZUGS 'DZIN ZHING, G-YON
PA'I KHU TSUR DKUR BRTEN PA DANG, BZANG SKYONG DKAR PO G-YAS PA
'BAR BA'I 'OD CAN GYI RIN PO CHE 'DZIN ZHING, G-YON PA'I KHU TSUR
DKUR BRTEN PA DANG DRA BA

DKAR PO PHYAG GNYIS KYIS YE SHES KYI BDUD RTZI'I BUM PA

PHYAG DAG GIS SNGO BSANGS LHA MO DANG SHIN TU BZANG MO DANG RTA
RNA BA DANG BYA GDONG MA DKAR MO RNAMS LA 'KHYUD PA'O, ,MI BSKYOD
PA'I GZHAL YAS KHANG GI DBUS SU GLANG PO CHE'I STENG DU SNA TSOGS
CHU SKYES DANG NYI MA LA KHYAB 'JUG GI SNYING GAR RDO RJE'I SKYIL
KRUNG GIS BZHUGS PA'I RDO RJE MKHA' 'GRO NAG PO STE RDO RJE DANG
RDO

RJES MTSAN PA'I DRIL BU 'DZIN PA'I G-YAS PA DANG G-YON PA'I PHYAG
DAG GIS RDO RJE MKHA' 'GRO MA LA 'KHYUD PA'O, ,DE NI DMAR MO'AM
NAG MO'O, ,SGO RNAMS LA STOBS PO CHE DANG RIN CHEN RDO RJE DANG
NAM MKHA'I SNYING PO RNAMS NI NAG PO STE RDO RJE DANG RDO RJE
DRIL BU 'DZIN PA'I PHYAG DAG GIS

@160B 'KHOR LO'I SHUGS CAN MA DANG DUM SKYES MA DANG CHANG 'TSONG
MA DANG 'KHOR LO'I GO CHA MA RNAMS SER MO LA 'KHYUD PA'O, ,DON
YOD GRUB PA'I GZHAL YAS KHANG GI DBUS SU NAM MKHA' LDING GI STENG
DU SNA TSOGS CHU SKYES DANG NYI MA LA GNAS PA'I LHA'I BU ZLA BA'I
SNYING GAR RDO RJE'I SKYIL KRUNG GIS BZHUGS

PA'I SNA TSOGS MKHA' 'GRO LJANG GU STE SNA TSOGS RDO RJES MTSAN
PA'I DRIL BU 'DZIN PA'I G-YAS PA DANG G-YON PA'I PHYAG DAG GIS
SNA TSOGS MKHA' 'GRO MA LJANG GU LA 'KHYUD PA'O, ,SGO RNAMS LA
DPAL HE RU KA DANG PADMA GAR GYI DBANG PHYUG DANG RNAM PAR SNANG
MDZAD DANG RDO RJE SEMS DPA' RNAMS LJANG

GU STE SNA TSOGS RDO RJE DANG SNA TSOGS RDO RJE'I DRIL BU 'DZIN
PA'I PHYAG DAG GIS SHIN TU DPA' MO DANG STOBS CHEN MO DANG 'KHOR
LOS SGYUR MA DANG BRTZON 'GRUS CHEN MO DU BA LTAR SNGO SKYA'I
MDOG CAN RNAMS LA 'KHYUD PA'O, ,DPA' BO NYI SHU RTZA BZHI NI
G-YAS BRKYANG GIS BZHUGS PA'O, ,'DIR MKHA'

'GRO MA LA SOGS PA NI G-YON PAS THOD PA DANG KHA tV'Am GA DANG
G-YAS PAS dA MA RU 'DZIN PA'O, ,YE SHES MKHA' 'GRO MA DANG RAB TU
GTUM MO LA SOGS PA BZHI NI PHYAG G-YAS PAS RDO RJE DANG BCAS PA'I
SDIGS MDZUB GDENGS PA'O, ,SANGS RGYAS MKHA' 'GRO MA DANG DPA'
BO'I BLO CAN MA LA SOGS

PA RNAMS NI 'KHOR LO DANG BCAS PA'I SDIGS MDZUB CAN NO, ,RIN CHEN
MKHA' 'GRO MA DANG SA SRUNG MA LA SOGS PA RNAMS NI RIN PO CHE
DANG BCAS PA'I SDIGS MDZUB PO, ,PADMA'I MKHA' 'GRO MA DANG BSNGO
BSANGS LHA MO LA SOGS PA RNAMS NI PADMA DANG BCAS PA'I SDIGS
MDZUB PO, ,RDO RJE MKHA' 'GRO DANG

'KHOR LO'I SHUGS CAN MA LA SOGS PA NI RDO RJE DANG BCAS PA'I
SDIGS MDZUB BO, ,SNA TSOGS MKHA' 'GRO MA DANG SHIN TU DPA' MO LA
SOGS PA RNAMS NI SNA TSOGS RDO RJE DANG BCAS PA'I SDIGS MDZUB BO,
,YE SHES MKHA' 'GRO MA LA SOGS PA THAMS CAD KYANG 'KHYUD PAR BYED
PA G-YON PA'I PHYAG DAG

GIS 'DZAG PA'I KHRAG GIS GANG BA'I THOD PA 'DZIN PA'O, ,DKYIL
'KHOR CHEN PO'I SGO RNAMS LA KHVA GDONG MA DANG 'UG GDONG MA DAD
KYI GDONG MA DANG PHAG GDONG MA RNAMS NI MING DANG RJES SU MTHUN
PA'I ZHAL CAN TE RIM PA JI LTA BAR SNGON MO DANG SER MO DANG DMAR
MO DANG LJANG GU'I MDOG CAN, PHYAG G-YAS

@161A *, ,PA RNAMS KYIS LCAGS KYU DANG ZHAGS PA DANG LCAGS SGROG
DANG DRIL BU 'DZIN PA'O, ,MTSAMS RNAMS LA GSHIN RJE BRTAN MA DANG
SHIN RJE PHO NYA MO DANG GSHIN RJE MCHE BA MA DANG GSHIN RJE
'JOMS MA RNAMS NI MI'I GDONG CAN TE, G-YAS DANG G-YON GYI SKU
PHYED PHYED G-YAS DANG G-YON GYI

LHA MO'I MDOG CAN, PHYAG G-YAS PA RNAMS KYIS ME LONG DANG PI WANG
DANG DRI'I DUNG CHOS DANG RO'I SNOD 'DZIN PA'O, ,LHA MO BRGYAD PO
'DI DAG KYANG G-YON PAS THOD PA DANG KHA tV'Am GA 'DZIN PA G-YAS
BRKYANG GIS GNAS PA'O, ,GZHAL YAS KHANG DRUG PO RNAMS KYI MTSAMS
RNAMS SU BYANG CHUB KYI SEMS LA

PA'O, ,MKHA' 'GRO MA LA SOGS PA NAS GSHIN RJE 'JOMS MA'I MTHAR

PA'O ZHES PA NI

PHYOGS GZHAN NO, ,LHA PHO RNAMS NI SKU RGYAB TU 'PHYANG BA'I STAG
GI PAGS PA'I SHAM THABS DKRIS PA, MCHOD PHYIR THOGS PA CAN MI MGO

MI MGO SKAM PO'I PHRENG BA

MGRIN PAR 'PHYANG BA'O, ,LHA MO BZHI BCU RTZA GNYIS PO RNAMS
KYANG ZHAL GCIG MA PHYAG GNYIS MA SPYAN GSUM PA RDO RJE PHRENG

RGYA LNGA DANG LDAN PA'O, ,'KHOR

NAG PA'I THOR COG CAN NO, ,LHA MO SUM CU RTZA BZHI PO RNAMS NI
RANG RANG GI 'KHOR LO'I DBANG PO LA MNGON PAR PHYOGS PA'O, ,'KHOR
LOS SGYUR BA LNGA DANG KHVA GDONG MA LA SOGS

PA RNAMS NI DBUS KYI 'KHOR LO'I DBANG PO LA MNGON PAR PHYOGS

DRUG PO 'DI DAG KYANG G-YAS BRKYANG GI ZHABS CAN NO ZHES PA'I
KHYAD PAR NI PHYOGS GNYIS

@161B PA'O, ,PHYOGS GNYIS PO 'DI DAG LA YANG YE SHES MKHA' 'GRO

@162A *, ,LAS THAMS CAD PA'I SNGAGS SO, ,DPAL DUS KYI 'KHOR LO LA

YUG RNAMS KYIS

@163A *, ,DE RNAMS KYANG SOR GDUB RNAMS KYI 'OD DANG LDAN PA'O,

@163B RNAMS KYIS GOS DANG SKA RAGS DANG RIN PO CHE'I RNA RGYAN

@164A *, ,PA RNAMS KYIS GZHU DANG ZHAGS PA DANG RIN PO CHE CHA

DBANG STE PHYIR MI LDOG PA NYID KYI SA BON NYID

KYANG BSKRUN PAR BYED PA'O, ,DE'I PHYIR DE LA LTOS NAS PHYIR MI
LDOG PAR BYA BA'I CHED DU DBANG BSKUR BA DANG, PHYIR MI LDOG PAR
BYE DPA'I DBANG BSKUR BA NI, PHYIR MI LDOG PA DANG LDAN PA'I
DBANG DANG PHYIR MI LDOG PA'I DBANG DU BRJOD DO, ,DE NYID KYI
PHYIR, RDO RJE GSANG BA YE SHES KYIS, ,SLOB DPON

ZHES BYA GSUM DU 'DOD, ,CES PA'I LUGS NI BLO GROS NGAN PA RNAMS
KHO NA'I YIN NO, ,'DI DAG LA SOGS PAS NI NYAN THOS KYI DAM TSIG
GIS RTZE BA SPANG BAR BYA'O ZHES PA'I NGES PA'I CHED DU, RDZOGS
PA'I SANGS RGYAS RDO RJE 'DZIN PAS RDO RJE LDAN CIG RAB TU SBYOR
BAS RTZE BAR BYA BA'I DON DU GANG GIS ME

TU RANG GI DAM TSIG LA MCHOD PAR BYA'O ZHES PA NI, PHRENG BA KUN
NAS 'PHANG BA'O, ,SEMS CAN THAMS CAD KYI BSAM PA JI LTA BA BZHIN
DU DAM PA'I CHOS YANG DAG PAR BRJOD PA'I DON DU AOm GYI YI GE
DANG SV'A'I YI GE KLOG PA'O, ,

DAG PAR 'BYOR ZHING, ,MTSAN

LA NI KHA'I TSAD GRUB ZHI BA'I SA LA CHA BCU GNYIS TE TSANGS THIG
GNYIS BTAB NAS TSANGS PA'I THIG

NAS BZUNG STE LTE BA NAS G-YAS DANG G-YON GYI ZUR JI SRID PAR
BSKOR ZHING TSANGS PA DANG ZUR GYI THIG GI MTHA' RNAMS PHYIS PA
LAS dA MA RUR 'GYUR RO, ,CHANGS PAS GZUNG BAR RANG PA'I SBOM PA
DANG RNA BA'I MTHAR THUG PAR RING BA NI YU BA STE GDONG GI TSAD
KYI GRUB ZHI'I SA LA SNGA MA BZHIN DU RTZE

MO GSUM PA'I RDO RJE YUL RE RER STENG DU BRKYANG BA LAS RTZE MO
GSUM DU 'GYUR RO, ,DE NAS KHA tV'Am GA NI DAM TSIG GI RDO RJE LTA
BU'I RDO RJES RTZE MOR RNAM PAR MDZES PA STE DE'I 'OG TU MI MOG
SKAM PO GSUM GYIS MDZES SHING SNA TSOGS RDO RJE DBUS SU BRGYAN
PA, RTZE MO GCIG PA'I RDO RJE GCIG

NI RTZA BA'I GNAS SU'O ZHES KHA CIG GO, ,DBYUG PA'I STENG DU SKAM
PO DANG RLON PA'I MI MGO GNYIS DANG DE'I SPYI BOR SNA TSOGS RDO
RJE DANG, DE'I LTE BAR BUM PA ZLUM PO 'DAB MA LA SOGS PAS KHA
BRGYAN PA DANG, KHA'I STENG DU DAM TSIG GI RDO RJE BA DANG LTAR
RAB TU 'PHYANG BA'O ZHES PA NI GNYIS

BA'O, ,GNYIS KA YANG YU BA'I STENG SBOM ZHING DBUS NAS PHRA BA
STE DRIL CHUNG LA SOGS PAS BRGYAN PA'O, ,MGO BO LA SOGS PA RNAMS
JI LTAR MDZES PAR BYA'O ZHES, MTHO'I TSAD GRU BZHI PA CHA BCU
GNYIS KYIS LA CHANG GZUNGS CHA BZHI NI DBUS SU'O, ,DE BZHIN DU
CHA BZHI NI 'KHYOG

DANG GDUGS DANG ZLA BA PHYED PA'I RNAM PA CAN GYI SGO SKYONG BYED
